### [104] [Fodor and Pylyshyn's Systematicity Challenge Still Stands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14512)
*Michael Goodale,Salvador Mascarenhas*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文批判了近期神经网络模型声称已解决人类认知系统性问题的观点，实验证明现有模型在系统性理解上仍存在重大缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期神经网络在自然语言处理上表现突出，引发认知科学界关注。有学者认为神经网络已解决Fodor和Pylyshyn提出的“系统性”难题，即人对句子理解存在系统性关联，但这一直是神经网络难以解释的现象。

Method: 论文主要复现并检验了Lake和Baroni提出的通过元学习促进组合性的神经网络模型，对比其在训练分布内外的系统性理解表现。

Result: 实验结果显示，该元学习模型在应对超出训练分布的句子时学习困难，在许多训练分布内的问题上也无法表现出人类一样的系统性、可逆性理解。

Conclusion: 作者认为，当前神经网络模型依然未能解决Fodor和Pylyshyn提出的认知系统性难题，关于神经网络能解释人类系统性理解的观点是过于乐观的。

Abstract: The recent successes of neural networks producing human-like language have caused significant stir in cognitive science, with many researchers arguing that classical puzzles about human cognition and challenges to artificial intelligence are being solved by neural networks. A notable case is the argument from systematicity due to Jerry Fodor and Zenon Pylyshyn, argues that humans display systematic biconditional dependencies. For example, someone can understand the sentence "John saw Mary" just in case that they understand the sentence "Mary saw John." Symbolic systems explain this systematicity of language and thought, while neural networks offer no immediate explanation. Several recent articles argue that this challenge has now been met by neural networks. In particular, Brenden Lake and Marco Baroni argue that their meta-learning for compositionality protocol matches and perhaps explains human systematicity. We demonstrate that these conclusions are premature. Among other results, we found that their model struggles to learn rules that are even slightly out of distribution compared to their training data. Furthermore, the model behaves unsystematically even on many within-distribution problems. We conclude that Fodor and Pylyshyn's challenge to neural networks remains unmet.

### [105] [BayLing-Duplex: Native Full-Duplex Speech Dialogue with a Single Autoregressive LLM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14528)
*Qingkai Fang,Shoutao Guo,Yang Feng*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的语音大模型多为回合制交互，严重依赖外部语音活动检测（VAD）模块限制了交互能力。需要一种能够实时、原生全双工对话的语音大模型。

Method: 提出BayLing-Duplex，将“是否听/说/停”等控制通过少量特殊tokens融入语言模型，无需改动原有架构即可集成于不同大模型，仅用约40万全双工样本微调并经过轻量化DPO（直接偏好优化）阶段。

Result: 在InstructS2S-Eval上，BayLing-Duplex实现了92%的回合判定成功率和100%的打断成功率，语音回复得分比基线模型Moshi（2.17分）提升至3.39分，在Llama Questions、Web Questions和Alpaca-Eval等通用问答任务上也保持或超越回合制系统表现。

Conclusion: BayLing-Duplex突破了传统语音大模型对回合检测模块的依赖，实现了高效、高质量的全双工语音交互，且不牺牲原有任务的回复质量。

Abstract: Real-time, full-duplex speech interaction is a key feature of next-generation spoken chatbots, allowing the model to listen and speak at the same time and to handle natural phenomena such as overlap, hesitation, and barge-in. Existing speech language models (SpeechLMs) such as LLaMA-Omni and GLM-4-Voice are still turn-based and rely on an external Voice Activity Detection (VAD) module to mark the end of the user's turn, which fundamentally limits their interactive ability. In this paper, we introduce BayLing-Duplex, a native full-duplex SpeechLM where a single autoregressive LLM decides when to listen, when to speak, and when to stop, with no auxiliary turn-taking module. The design adds only a few special tokens to the standard vocabulary, so it transfers across LLMs and reuses existing training and serving stacks with no architectural adaptation. Starting from the public GLM-4-Voice checkpoint and using only 400K full-duplex samples for fine-tuning followed by a lightweight DPO stage, BayLing-Duplex reaches 92% turn-taking success and 100% interruption success on InstructS2S-Eval, while improving the speech-response score from 2.17 to 3.39 over Moshi. BayLing-Duplex also matches or surpasses its turn-based counterpart on Llama Questions, Web Questions, and Alpaca-Eval, showing that simultaneous listen-and-speak modeling does not sacrifice response quality.

### [106] [SIMMER: Benchmarking Latent Failures in LLM Executable Planning with a World Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14574)
*Xiaoxin Lu,Ranran Haoran Zhang,Rui Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了SIMMER基准，用于评测大语言模型（LLM）在家庭环境任务规划中的潜在失败，尤其关注那些不易被即时检测到但会影响任务完成甚至造成不可逆后果的潜在失误。实验显示主流LLM表现存在显著不足，但通过状态推理和反事实模拟可显著减少此类失误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM任务规划评测大多只关注计划是否能被成功执行，忽略了执行过程中未能即时暴露但危及目标实现的潜在失误，这在实际场景（如厨房任务）中可能导致严重后果，因此需要系统性评测与研究。

Method: 作者构建了SIMMER基准，在厨房符号世界模型下设计77种操作、262个对象和约46800种交互，用状态机执行器自动检测计划的即时失败、潜在风险及不可逆结果，并且对六种主流LLM进行了系统评测，同时探索了基于反事实模拟的状态推理方法来减少潜在失败。

Result: 即便是最前沿的LLM，完全无错误计划的比例也仅有17%。高达56%的计划包含潜在失误，其中多数导致不可逆后果。通过显式状态推理和反事实模拟，潜在失误可减少72%，不可逆失误减少75%。

Conclusion: 现有LLM在复杂家庭任务规划中存在大量潜在失误，常被传统评测忽视。通过更细致的状态推理与对未来情境的模拟，能大幅提升LLM计划的安全性与鲁棒性，未来可据此优化与发展更健壮的规划系统。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as planners for autonomous agents in household environments. While existing benchmarks evaluate whether LLM-generated plans execute successfully, they overlook a critical type of failure: latent failures. Unlike immediate failures that trigger instant feedback at execution time and enable timely correction, latent failures do not immediately halt plan execution but silently compromise goal achievement. In severe cases, they cause irreversible harm. To address this gap, we introduce SIMMER, a benchmark for evaluating latent failures in LLM planning through a human-curated symbolic world model grounded in the kitchen domain. SIMMER defines a world model comprising 77 actions, 262 unique objects, and approximately 46,800 possible interactions that are semantically realistic, derived from real-world cooking scripts. It then leverages a state machine executor that validates plans against the world model and detects immediate precondition violations, latent hazards, and irreversible failures. Experiments across six LLMs show that even frontier models achieve at most 17% error-free plans. Moreover, up to 56% of plans contain latent failures, the majority of which lead to irreversible consequences. We further demonstrate that explicit state reasoning via counterfactual foresight simulation can reduce latent failures by up to 72% and irreversible cases by up to 75%, suggesting a promising direction for more robust LLM planners.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者提出了PI体系，基于心理学和传播学中的说服理论，设计了15个主维度和55个子特征，并用词表和规则检测方法实现。该体系具有模块化结构，可以替换单个检测器而不影响理论结构。通过在四个风格多样、领域不同的公开数据集上评估PI的有效性，结合线性模型展示特征的预测能力和计算效率。

Abstract: Identifying persuasive rhetorical cues is critical across domains, from detecting information manipulation and improving AI safety to advancing public health communication. We propose Persuasion Index (PI), a taxonomy of 15 dimensions grounded in persuasion theories from psychology and communication, and one transparent implementation using 55 sub-features built from lexicons and rule-based detectors. The taxonomy is modular: individual detectors can be replaced while preserving the theoretical structure. By evaluating PI on four public datasets varying in domain, style, and outcome measures, we show that PI provides a shared feature space for interpreting rhetorical patterns associated with persuasion-related outcomes. Linear models show that PI features carry meaningful predictive signal while remaining computationally lightweight. Dimension-level analyses reveal recurring associations between PI dimensions and persuasion outcomes across datasets, while also highlighting topic- and stance-specific variation. We release PI as an open-source package and web interface for principled and auditable analysis of human and AI-mediated communication.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前在线群聊存在隐含的本地对话规范，但这些规范很少被明示。现有LLM是否能识别并适应这些规范尚未得到深入研究。

Method: 作者设计了LoSoNA基准：为被测模型提供包含隐含社交规范的群聊记录和引导性提问，通过其反应判断其对规范的推断能力。共评测了八个主流开源与闭源模型，并设置四种不同的提示方式（prompting），分析不同提示对模型表现的影响。

Abstract: Online group chats are social spaces with local conversational norms that are rarely stated explicitly. The ability and willingness of LLM-based agents to recognize and adapt to these norms remains mostly unexplored. We introduce LoSoNA, a benchmark for local social norm adaptation in multi-party chat. Each scenario gives a subject model a curated group-chat transcript in which non-subject participants demonstrate a hidden local norm, followed by a final elicitor turn that forces a response revealing whether the subject has inferred that norm. We evaluate eight frontier and open-weight models under four prompting conditions that vary how explicitly the model is told to treat the prior conversation as evidence for how it should answer. Naive prompting remains limited for most models; explicit norm-aware prompting helps unevenly, with Gemini 3.1 Pro reaching $84.2\%$ and Claude Fable 5 reaching $81.6\%$, while several other models show small gains or regressions. LoSoNA contributes to recent calls for evaluating LLM social capabilities by testing whether models can infer local conversational norms from precedent and use them in a one-turn group-chat response.

### [109] [Characterizing Cultural Localization in AI-Generated Stories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14626)
*Shaily Bhatt,Supriti Vijay,Jeremiah Milbauer,Fernando Diaz*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种衡量故事内容文化本地化方式的新方法，揭示了许多AI生成故事主要依赖模板化的文化标记，并分析了这些标记的刻板性和冒犯性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着人工智能的全球应用，如何评价其生成文化本地化内容（如故事）的能力已成为热门课题。现有内容本地化常通过简单替换文化标记（如人名、地名），而不是深入调整叙事结构及价值观，缺乏对两者差异的衡量方法，因此需要新的评估手段。

Method: 作者提出新方法，通过识别区分不同国别故事的词汇，并在移除这些文化标记后，比较剩余叙事的相似性。研究涵盖5种生成模型、125个主题、193个国别。

Result: 结果显示，仅9-17%的词汇解释了国别间的叙事差异。在移除这些词汇后，叙事内容之间存在大量重复短语，说明AI更偏向于用通用模板填充故事。此外，对文化标记的分析发现，来源于全球南方19个国家的标记平均更具冒犯性。

Conclusion: 大多数AI生成故事依赖于模板化的本地化方式，未实现更深层次的文化适应。所提方法能有效区分模板化与整体性本地化，对内容本地化的评估和风险规避有指导意义。

Abstract: The global use of artificial intelligence has increased interest in assessing the ability to generate culturally localized content, including stories. Cultural localization in stories often occurs through either templated localization -- the use of cultural markers (e.g., names, locations) in a generic narrative -- or holistic localization -- the variation of plots, values, and themes, in addition to cultural markers. We propose a method to measure the degree to which content was generated through templated localization. Specifically, we identify the lexical tokens that distinguish stories across nationalities and measure the similarity of the narratives that remain after removing them. In stories generated by five models on 125 topics for 193 nationalities, our method is able to detect that only a small subset (9-17%) of the vocabulary accounts for the variation across nationalities and that the narratives that remain after removing them contain repeated multi-word sequences, suggesting the presence of a shared culturally-agnostic narrative template. Finally, we characterize the cultural markers for their stereotypicality and offensiveness, finding that markers from 19 countries, mostly located in the Global South, are on average offensive.

### [110] [AgentSpec: Understanding Embodied Agent Scaffolds Through Controlled Composition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14674)
*Jixuan Chen,Jianzhi Shen,Haoqiang Kang,Zhi Hong,Qingyi Jiang,Soham Bose,Yiming Zhang,Leon Leng,Amit Vyas,Lingjun Mao,Siru Ouyang,Kun Zhou,Lianhui Qin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种名为AgentSpec的模块化规范框架，用于标准化和组合大型语言模型（LLM）智能体的各功能模块，并通过多种环境验证了该框架的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM智能体多由多模块搭建，但模块高度耦合，难以独立评估、比较组件设计或理解模块间的影响，限制了创新和工程可扩展性。

Method: 提出AgentSpec框架，将智能体各组件（感知、记忆、推理、反思、行动与强化学习等）标准化定义为可复用的策略模块，通过标准接口组合，实现按需替换与对比实验，并在多种具身智能体基准（DeliveryBench, ALFRED, MiniGrid, RoboTHOR）上具体实现并分析。

Result: 实验发现，智能体性能主要取决于模块间兼容性与交互效应，而不仅仅是单个模块性能。多层次记忆结构提升长时跟踪能力；推理与记忆在不同环境下交互不同；反思可平衡修正和成本；基于RL训练的策略与实际部署结构相适配时表现最佳。

Conclusion: AgentSpec为构建、分析和对比可组合LLM智能体提供了标准化、可控的平台，促进了智能体系统的模块复用与创新，对未来复杂智能体架构研究具有重要意义。

Abstract: LLM agents are increasingly built not as single model calls, but as scaffolded systems that combine reasoning, memory, reflection, action execution, and learning. While such scaffolds often improve performance, they are often embedded in tightly coupled pipelines, making it difficult to isolate component contributions, compare alternative designs, or understand how module interactions shape agent behavior. We introduce AgentSpec, a modular specification framework that represents embodied agents as typed compositions of reusable policy components with standardized interfaces. AgentSpec standardizes the interfaces among perception, memory, reasoning, reflection, action, and optional learning, enabling components to be swapped and recombined under controlled conditions. We instantiate this framework across DeliveryBench, ALFRED, MiniGrid, and RoboTHOR, and analyze reasoning, memory, reflection, and reinforcement-learning modules across model backbones. Our results show that agent performance is governed by scaffold compatibility and interaction effects rather than isolated module strength. In particular, structured multi-granularity memory improves long-horizon state tracking, reasoning and memory interact non-uniformly across environments, reflection trades off correction and cost, and RL-trained policies compose best when optimized with deployment-time scaffold structure. AgentSpec provides a controlled foundation for studying, comparing, and designing composable LLM agents. Our code, baselines and interactive playground are publicly available at https://agentspec-embodied.github.io.

</details>


### [111] [CORA: Analyzing and bridging thinking-answer gap in Multimodal RLVR via Consistency-Oriented Reasoning Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14691)
*Jiayue Cao,Zhicong Lu,Xuehan Sun,Wei Jia,Hongling Zheng,Changyuan Tian,Zichuan Lin,Wenqian Lv,Nayu Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种面向一致性的多模态大模型推理强化学习方法CORA，提升了模型的推理与答案一致性，并增强了任务表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态大模型中的强化学习方法（RLVR）虽然能提升模型的视觉推理能力，但容易忽视推理过程与最终答案之间的语义不一致问题，影响了模型的合理性和信任度，因此需对该问题进一步研究和改进。

Method: 作者提出了一种新的方法CORA（Consistency-Oriented Reasoning Alignment），在RLVR流程中引入轻量级的一致性奖励模型，专注于推理与答案的语义一致性。同时结合了Hybrid Reward Advantage Splitting (HRAS) 机制，协同优化任务表现和语义一致性。方法适用于主流多模态推理基准和各类大规模视觉-语言模型。

Result: 实验结果显示，CORA不仅提升了推理任务的表现，还有效缓解了推理过程与最终答案不一致的问题，推理链条更加真实可信。

Conclusion: 引入一致性认知机制到多模态RLVR流程能有效提升模型推理的可靠性与表现，为后续多模态大模型推理方法提供了新的方向。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has successfully elicited the reasoning capabilities of large language models, motivating its extension to multimodal scenarios. Existing methods primarily focus on improving the visual coverage of reasoning traces and mitigating visual hallucinations, but underestimate the semantic inconsistency between the reasoning process and the final answer. In this paper, we delve into thinking-answer inconsistency in RLVR for large vision-language models (LVLMs), showing thorough analyses of rollouts collected throughout Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) training process and post-RLVR evaluation outputs that this issue persists during training and remains present during inference. Motivated by the analysis, we propose Consistency-Oriented Reasoning Alignment (CORA), which introduces thinking-answer semantic consistency into RLVR through a lightweight plug-and-play consistency reward model, and further incorporates Hybrid Reward Advantage Splitting (HRAS) to stably coordinate task and consistency optimization. Extensive experiments across representative multimodal reasoning benchmarks and mainstream LVLMs show that CORA improves task performance while effectively mitigating thinking-answer inconsistency, leading to more faithful reasoning traces.

</details>


### [112] [AdaSR: Adaptive Streaming Reasoning with Hierarchical Relative Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14694)
*Junlong Tong,Wenqi Xu,Yingqi Fan,Anhao Zhao,Xuan Lu,Yang Tan,Xiaoyu Shen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种自适应流式推理框架AdaSR，能在输入流过程中进行推理，并在输入完成后进行最终决策，相较现有主流方法在准确性、效率和延迟间实现更优平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大模型主要采用读-后-思策略，无法适应信息流动态变化（如音视频流等场景），且已有流式推理方法高度依赖人工监督轨迹，灵活性受限。

Method: 提出AdaSR框架，在输入流阶段进行推理，待输入结束后进行深度思考；并引入层次化相对策略优化方法（HRPO），分别优化流式与深度推理阶段，结合格式、准确性和自适应思考奖励，鼓励模型动态分配计算。

Result: 实验结果表明，AdaSR在推理准确率、计算效率和流式延迟方面均优于基线的有监督微调方法。

Conclusion: AdaSR为应对动态流式输入任务提供了更具自适应性的推理方案，兼顾准确性与效率，对实际流式场景具有较高应用价值。

Abstract: Large reasoning models typically follow a read-then-think paradigm: they observe the complete input, reason over a static context, and then produce the answer. Yet many real-world scenarios are inherently dynamic, such as audio and video stream, where information arrives as a continuous stream and models must reason, update, and respond under partial observations. Recent streaming reasoning methods allow models to think while reading, but they largely rely on supervised imitation of pre-constructed trajectories, which limits their flexibility. In this paper, we propose AdaSR, an adaptive streaming reasoning framework that enables models to reason during input streaming and perform final deliberation once the stream is complete, learning when to think, and how much computation to allocate across different stages. To optimize this hierarchical reasoning process, we introduce Hierarchical Relative Policy Optimization (HRPO), which decomposes policy optimization into streaming reasoning and deep reasoning phases, providing more fine-grained advantage assignment instead of uniformly distributing a single sequence-level advantage over all tokens. HRPO integrates format, accuracy, and adaptive thinking rewards to enforce valid reasoning protocols, preserve final task performance, and encourage latency-aware computation allocation. Experiments show that AdaSR achieves a better balance among reasoning accuracy, computational efficiency, and streaming latency compared with supervised fine-tuning baseline. We release our code at https://github.com/EIT-NLP/StreamingLLM/tree/main/AdaSR.

</details>

### [113] [Occupancy-Grounded Room Segmentation for Hierarchical 3D Scene Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13727)
*Carlos Cueto Zumaya,Iacopo Catalano,Jorge Peña-Queralta,Wallace Moreira Bessa*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种基于空间占用（occupancy-grounded）的3D场景图（3DSG）生成管线，将室内的房间节点锚定为显式多边形，从而提升房间区域的识别效果，并在Matterport3D数据集上取得了优于现有方法的召回效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前室内机器人常用的3D场景图在房间层建立上有多种空间划分基准，导致各方法间评价标准不一致，且难以精确匹配真实房间的几何结构，需要更一致且几何明确的方法。

Method: 提出以占用分解得到的自由空间区域为依据，为每个房间节点分配明确的多边形边界，形成占用锚定的3DSG。通过将预测的房间多边形与实际标注房间进行匹配，并与现有的Hydra方法进行对比评测。

Result: 该方法比基于“点连接(place-connectivity)”的建图方式在房间实例召回率上有明显提升，但精度有所下降。两种方法在房间边界的精确度上都存在不足。

Conclusion: 占用分解锚定的3DSG方法能更全面地还原房间实例，为室内场景图的构建提供了更好的方案，但高精度的墙体边界划分仍待进一步研究。

Abstract: Hierarchical 3D scene graphs (3DSGs) for indoor robots organize geometric and semantic information across spatial scales, with a room layer that connects object-level perception to room-scale reasoning. Existing systems construct this layer from different spatial substrates (\eg{} place clusters, wall planes, or segmentation outputs), and as a result, room nodes are not evaluated on a common geometric criterion. We present an occupancy-grounded 3DSG pipeline in which room nodes are anchored to tracked free-space regions derived from occupancy decomposition, giving each room an explicit polygonal footprint. We evaluate the pipeline on 12 Matterport3D scenes by matching predicted room polygons to annotated room instances and compare against Hydra, a representative state-of-the-art place-connectivity baseline. The results show that occupancy-grounded anchoring recovers substantially more room instances than place-connectivity construction, at the cost of lower precision, and that wall-accurate room boundaries remain an open problem for both methods. Code is available at https://github.com/crcz25/OccuSG.

</details>


### [114] [Scalable Dynamic Tactile Sensing Enabled by Passive and Flexible Acoustic Waveguides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13746)
*Guimin Long,Changhong Linghu,Chuanping Liu,Ke Xu,Xingjian Jing*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新型的基于深亚波长声波导的被动分布式动态触觉传感阵列，具有高灵敏度、高鲁棒性和柔性，可大范围应用于人机界面。通过弹性膜封盖赫姆霍兹共振腔及弹簧加固微管网络，实现了在系统宏观弯曲下的稳定传感，并可低成本大面积扩展。实验展示了多种原型（指尖、手套、大面积皮肤）对极微弱触觉刺激的精准检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前动态触觉传感技术在扩展到大面积阵列时常面临灵敏度、柔顺性、鲁棒性以及连接线复杂和成本高昂的权衡，亟需开发一种兼具性能与可扩展性的解决方案。

Method: 设计了一种被动分布式声学传感网络，由弹性膜封盖的赫姆霍兹共振腔和微管组成，腔体间相连并可在宏观弯曲情况下实现不变声学传递。通过稀疏嵌入麦克风和基于连续小波变换+轻量神经网络，实现对低频（<100 Hz）信号的实时定位和波形重构。

Result: 在仅布置4个麦克风的64节点感测阵列中，空间分辨率最高可达4毫米，准确率大于99%；推理时延仅5.5毫秒。原型可检测单根毛发、5毫克颗粒冲击、动脉脉搏、羽毛触碰等微弱刺激。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了可扩展、柔性、低成本的下一代大面积动态触觉传感阵列范式，为人机界面技术带来新突破。

Abstract: Artificial dynamic tactile sensing requires sensitivity, robustness, and compliance, yet existing technologies face trade-offs when scaling to large-area arrays, compounded by wiring complexity and cost. Here, we report a passive distributed paradigm using deep sub-wavelength acoustic waveguides that decouples performance from structural flexibility. Elastic-membrane-capped Helmholtz resonators interconnected by spring-reinforced microtubes form an enclosed network with invariant acoustic transmission under macroscopic bending. By sparsely embedding microphones, the system achieves real-time localization (4 mm highest spatial resolution; >99% accuracy in a 4 microphones 64-node sensing array) and waveform reconstruction of low-frequency signals (<100 Hz). Fast Continuous Wavelet Transform and a lightweight neural network enable inference within 5.5 ms. We demonstrate conformable prototypes-fingertip arrays, a tactile glove, and large-area skins-detecting stimuli from single-hair contact to 5-mg particle impacts, arterial pulse waves, feather touches, and finger contact. This establishes a scalable, flexible, low-cost paradigm for next-generation human-machine interfaces.

</details>


### [115] [$μ_0$: A Scalable 3D Interaction-Trace World Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13769)
*Seungjae Lee,Yoonkyo Jung,Jusuk Lee,Jonghun Shin,Amir Hossein Shahidzadeh,Yao-Chih Lee,H. Jin Kim,Jia-Bin Huang,Furong Huang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种基于3D轨迹的通用世界模型μ_0，可以不依赖具体机器人动作标签，实现可扩展的学习和迁移，显著优于传统像素级视频模型和直接动作建模方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界模型要么依赖密集像素重建，效率较低；要么需要具体机器人动作标签，限制了可扩展性和跨平台通用性。因此需要一种既紧凑高效又脱离具体动作标签的物理世界表征方法。

Method: 作者提出了μ_0模型，通过预测交互物体、工具、手、接触点等关键点在3D空间的平滑轨迹，实现对物理运动的抽象建模。为训练这种模型，设计了TraceExtract系统，从多样的视频中自动提取3D关键点轨迹，并结合层次化的语言描述进行有监督预训练。μ_0结合了预训练视觉-语言骨干网络和模块化轨迹专家，以B样条控制点表示轨迹，预测未来运动。

Result: 实验表明μ_0在2D和3D轨迹预测任务中显著超过现有轨迹预测和VLM（视觉-语言模型）方法，而且μ_0冻结后可与不同动作专家组合，迁移到不同机器人。其轨迹条件策略在无需动作监督的前提下，达到与动作监督模型（如π_0）接近的性能。

Conclusion: 基于3D轨迹的运动表征是一种高效、可扩展且易于迁移的方法，有望成为跨机器人平台操作的新基础表征。该工作为无需具体动作标签的机器人学习和泛化提供了有前景的方向。

Abstract: World models that capture how actions induce physical change enable scalable robot learning without reliance on embodiment-specific action labels. Pixel-space video models provide broad visual priors but expend model capacity on dense appearance reconstruction, while direct action models require embodiment-specific labels that hinder scalability. We present $μ_0$, a scalable world model based on 3D traces. Rather than predicting dense pixels or directly modeling actions, $μ_0$ forecasts smooth 3D trajectories for salient interaction points such as objects, tools, hands, and contact regions, yielding a compact, embodiment-agnostic motion interface. To enable training from diverse video sources, our TraceExtract system automatically extracts 3D supervision by selecting keypoints, constructing globally aligned traces, and associating motion segments with hierarchical language captions. This TraceExtract supervision pretrains $μ_0$ by combining a pretrained vision-language backbone with a modular trace expert, which represents each query via B-spline control points and predicts future traces. Experiments show that $μ_0$ outperforms baselines in both 2D and 3D trace prediction, including trace prediction models and tokenized VLM methods. Because $μ_0$ is frozen and reusable, it can be paired with action experts for downstream robot embodiments. Despite action-free pretraining, the resulting trace-conditioned policies achieve performance competitive with VLA models pretrained with action supervision, such as $π_0$. These results establish 3D traces as a scalable and transferable representation for cross-embodiment manipulation.

</details>


### [116] [FlowMo-WM: A World Model with Object Momentum and Hidden Ambient Drift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13817)
*Yitao Jiang,Luyang Zhao,Muhao Chen,Devin Balkcom*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了FlowMo-WM，一个可端到端训练的视觉世界模型，能够在没有流场直接监督的情况下，推断目标运动状态和与环境隐性漂移相关的长历史上下文，从而在含有水流等扰动环境中提升长期预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人世界模型多评估于即时控制起主导作用的环境，但现实水面机器人等物体同时受惯性和不可见的环境漂移影响（如水流、风），导致现有模型预测精度不高。因此需开发能同时建模自身动力学和外部扰动影响的世界模型。

Method: FlowMo-WM通过将图像-动作历史分解为短期潜在状态（表示目标中心运动）和长期上下文（表示缓变外源影响），并采用无监督地从历史中推断流场和漂移影响。模型中用零上下文残差变换将与动作相关的基础动力学和与环境上下文相关的漂移效应区分开。

Result: 在含有多样隐性水流、干扰和随机化动力学的仿真水面机器人环境下，FlowMo-WM在长期预测精度上优于典型有动作条件的潜在世界模型。通过置零或扰乱上下文的消融实验，证明环境上下文对隐藏漂移条件下的稳定预测至关重要。同时用冻结的线性探针分析了模型所学表示信息。

Conclusion: FlowMo-WM有效建模并分离了机器人自主运动与外部环境隐性漂移的影响，提升了含有隐藏流场环境下的长期世界预测能力，对复杂扰动场景下的机器人智能决策和控制具有重要意义。

Abstract: World models in robot learning predict future states from visual observations and actions, enabling agents to reason about the consequences of their controls. However, many action-conditioned models are evaluated in settings where motion is dominated by immediate control, whereas aquatic surface vehicles and other real-world objects continue moving under inertia and are displaced by hidden ambient drift, such as water currents or wind. We propose FlowMo-WM, an end-to-end trainable visual world model that infers object-centric motion state and a predictive long-history context associated with hidden drift from image-action histories without direct supervision of flow fields. FlowMo-WM factorizes image-action history into a short-history latent state, trained to summarize object-centric motion, and a longer-history context, trained to summarize slowly varying exogenous influences. A zero-context residual transition separates action-conditioned base dynamics from context-dependent drift effects during latent rollout. In simulated aquatic surface-vehicle environments with diverse hidden flows, disturbances, and randomized vehicle dynamics, FlowMo-WM improves long-horizon rollout accuracy over representative action-conditioned latent world models. Prediction-time context ablations, in which the inferred context is zeroed or shuffled during rollout, show that the ambient context is important for stable prediction under hidden drift, while frozen linear probes characterize information encoded in the learned factors.

</details>

*Senkang Hu,Zhengru Fang,Yihang Tao,Zihan Fang,Sam Tak Wu Kwong,Yuguang Fang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本综述聚焦于自动驾驶领域从单车智能向多智能体协作系统的转变，系统梳理了共享世界模型（SWMs）的相关研究进展与挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动驾驶逐步演变为多主体系统，强调在不确定环境下车辆之间的协作与信息共享，以提升交通效率与安全。为此需系统梳理当前共享世界模型及其在多主体自动驾驶中的应用难点。

Method: 通过回顾超过380篇相关文献，涵盖V2X通信、协同感知、智能体认知、协同规划、端到端协作驾驶和闭环验证等领域，分析信息如何从观测共享转化为状态对齐、意图理解与协作行动。

Result: 目前多主体协同主要停留在仿真、标准数据集和离线评测阶段，实际开放环境中缺乏实时安全保障，尤其是大模型驱动下的协作机制。

Conclusion: 未来研究需聚焦可验证的共享状态维护、鲁棒的意图和计划对齐，以及在通信、时延和部署受限下的安全协作行动，以推动多智能体自动驾驶实际落地。

Abstract: Autonomous driving is shifting from isolated vehicle intelligence toward multi-agent embodied systems that share perception, infer intent, and coordinate action under uncertainty. This survey examines this transition through the lens of Shared World Models (SWMs): predictive cross-agent representations maintained across vehicles, infrastructure, and other traffic participants. We review more than 380 publications spanning vehicle-to-everything (V2X) communication, collaborative perception, inter-agent cognition, cooperative planning, end-to-end cooperative driving, and simulation and data engines for closed-loop validation. The organizing question is how exchanged observations become aligned state, intent-aware interaction, and coordinated downstream action. Across the surveyed literature, evaluation remains concentrated in simulation, curated benchmarks, and offline protocols. Foundation-model-based coordination also lacks verified real-time safety guarantees in open traffic. These gaps motivate key research priorities for multi-agent embodied autonomous driving (MAEAD): verifiable shared-state maintenance, robust intent and plan alignment, and safe coordinated action under communication, latency, and deployment constraints.

</details>


### [118] [Efficient Domain-Adaptive Policy Learning via Kernel Representation with Application to Quadrotor Control under Non-Stationary Disturbances](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13842)
*Hongyu Zhou,Mingtian Tan,Vasileios Tzoumas*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于核表示的高效领域自适应策略学习算法，实现了对复杂扰动环境下的无人机（如四旋翼）轨迹跟踪任务的快速自适应和高效训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 领域自适应策略学习面临需要模型既具备表达复杂仿真-现实差距的能力，又要支持在线快速自适应的挑战。特别在无人机如四旋翼应用中，环境扰动多变且非平稳，例如风、载荷突变和地效切换，这对现有策略适应性和算法效率都提出了很高要求。

Method: 论文用可微分的随机傅里叶特征核逼近来建模环境扰动。在离线训练阶段，随机采样核参数生成多样扰动，以可微分仿真和解析梯度优化控制策略（训练仅需50秒，硬件平台为RTX 4090 GPU）。在线部署阶段，策略通过最小二乘法动态更新核参数，实现实时适应复杂非平稳扰动。

Result: 该方法在高保真数值仿真和实际Crazyflie无人机上的多种复杂扰动（气动效应、风、地效、载荷变化等）下进行了评估，实验验证了其轨迹跟踪任务上的高效适应性和优秀性能。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于核的领域自适应策略学习方法兼具高效性和强表达力，能够实现对复杂扰动环境下的无人机快速自适应控制，实验效果优良，对仿真到现实的强化学习迁移具有重要意义。

Abstract: We present an algorithm for efficient domain-adaptive policy learning via kernel representations. Learning domain-adaptive policies is challenging since it requires an environment representation that is both sufficiently expressive to model complex sim-to-real gaps during offline training, and computationally efficient enough to support rapid online adaptation during deployment. For instance, a quadrotor may encounter time-varying, non-stationary disturbances, such as sudden gusts of wind, payload shifts, or transitions between distinct flight regimes with and without ground effects. To address these challenges, we model unknown disturbances using a differentiable kernel approximation based on random Fourier features. During the offline training phase, we randomly sample kernel coefficients and bandwidth parameters to generate a rich diversity of disturbance profiles. We then optimize the control policy via differentiable simulation with analytical gradients, a process that takes only 50 seconds of training time on an RTX 4090 GPU. During hardware deployment, the policy adapts to non-stationary environments in real time by updating both the kernel coefficients and bandwidth through online least-squares estimation. We evaluate our method on quadrotor trajectory tracking tasks across high-fidelity numerical simulations and hardware experiments using Crazyflie, subjected to various disturbances, including complex aerodynamic effects, wind, ground effects, and payload fluctuations.

</details>


### [119] [Output-Level Regularization Eliminates the Seed Lottery in Single-GPU VLA Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13856)
*Jeffrin Sam,Dzmitry Tsetserukou*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文发现，微调视觉-语言-动作模型（VLA-JEPA）时，不同随机种子会导致显著性能波动，这种“种子彩票”现象可能使模型性能从91%骤降至65%。作者追踪原因，发现是输出层坍塌，现有权重层面正则化无法避免。通过输出层正则化（如VICReg、Dropout、减半学习率）可有效避免该问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前微调多模态模型如VLA-JEPA应当易于复现与部署，但作者发现在完全相同的训练设置下，更换随机种子会导致一次训练结果严重失效。该现象在实际机器人推理场景下无预警发生，亟需定位与解决。

Method: 作者系统地对比了多种正则化策略（权重层面和输出层面），并利用Jacobian零空间理论分析模型坍塌机制，分别在3个基准任务和多种随机种子下进行实验。重点考察了VICReg、Dropout和学习率调整等简单方法对输出坍塌的影响。

Result: 输出层正则化方法（VICReg、Dropout、减半学习率）在所有实验设定下完全消除模型输出坍塌现象，而传统的权重层面方法（L2、EWC）无效。用最简单的输出正则化就能解决29个百分点性能骤降的风险。

Conclusion: 微调大模型时，输出坍塌会导致“种子彩票”风险。权重正则化不足以解决，推荐用输出层正则化（如VICReg、Dropout、调整学习率），只需简单配置即可大幅提升稳定性，避免严重性能损失。

Abstract: Fine-tuning a vision-language-action model (VLA-JEPA) on a single GPU should be simple: load a pretrained checkpoint, run training, deploy. There is a hidden danger. Run the same fine-tuning code thirteen times -- same data, same architecture, different random seed -- and twelve runs produce a robot succeeding 91--94% of the time, while one run silently degrades to 65.2%: a 29 pp gap with no error message, no warning, and no way to predict which seed will fail. We call this the seed lottery. We trace the cause to output collapse: the action predictor quietly learns to produce nearly identical outputs regardless of what the robot sees. Existing weight-level methods (L2, EWC) are structurally blind to this collapse -- they penalize weight changes, but collapse occurs in directions weights can move freely without affecting outputs, a gap we formalize via the Jacobian null-space. Across 7 methods x up to 13 seeds x 3 LIBERO benchmarks, three output-level regularizers -- VICReg (n=12 seeds), Dropout (n=4), and a halved learning rate (n=5) -- each eliminate every catastrophic seed (0/21 combined collapses vs. 1/13 Baseline; F(12,11)=28.7, p<0.001), while weight-level methods (L2, EWC) preserve the lottery. The simplest fix is changing one number in your optimizer config.

</details>


### [120] [ContactWorld: What Matters in Vision-Tactile World Models for Contact-Rich Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13877)
*Zhiyuan Zhang,Pokuang Zhou,Kaidi Zhang,Adeesh Desai,Temitope Amosa,Davood Soleymanzadeh,Jiuzhou Lei,Minghui Zheng,Yu She*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了ContactWorld基准，系统研究了视觉-触觉世界模型在12种接触密集操纵任务中的表现，发现具有空间结构和时间连续性的表达能显著提升长期规划性能，点云和触觉力场表现尤佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 接触丰富的机器人操作需要世界模型应对复杂的多模态观测下的接触动力学。目前尚不清楚哪些表达特性对于实现稳定的长期规划至关重要。

Method: 作者提出ContactWorld基准，涵盖插入、拆卸、螺旋和探索等12种任务，通过大量实验，系统比较了不同视觉（如点云、单目）和触觉（如力场）观测下的世界模型表达特性对规划性能的影响。

Result: 空间结构化和时间连续性的表达显著提升了规划成功率。其中点云观测将成功率提高到32.1%，点云与触觉力场结合进一步提升至36.1%。此外，触觉在长时规划中变得更为关键。

Conclusion: 高质量的表达结构、多模态兼容性和长期鲁棒性对提升机器人在接触密集任务中的规划性能至关重要，特别是在融合点云和触觉力场时效果最佳。

Abstract: Contact-rich manipulation requires world models to reason over complex contact dynamics from multimodal sensory observations. However, it remains unclear which representation properties fundamentally support stable long-horizon planning in contact-rich settings. In this paper, we present ContactWorld, a benchmark and systematic empirical study of vision-tactile world models spanning 12 contact-rich manipulation tasks, including insertion, disassembly, screwing, and exploratory interaction. Across extensive experiments, we find that representations that are both spatially structured and temporally continuous consistently achieve the strongest planning performance. In particular, point-cloud observations improve average planning success rates from 20.7% with wrist-view observations and 22.0% with front-view observations to 32.1%. We further find that the effectiveness of tactile sensing depends critically on cross-modal representation compatibility rather than modality scaling alone. Combining point-cloud observations with tactile force-field representations, which preserve richer spatial structure and interaction dynamics, further improves performance to 36.1%, yielding the strongest overall planning performance across all evaluated tasks. Moreover, tactile sensing becomes increasingly important under long-horizon planning objectives, where compounding prediction errors and contact uncertainty accumulate over time. Together, these findings highlight the importance of representation structure, multimodal compatibility, and long-horizon robustness in vision-tactile world models for contact-rich robotic manipulation.

### [121] [AnyGoal: Vision-Language Guided Multi-Agent Exploration for Training-Free Lifelong Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13878)
*MoniJesu James,Marcelino Julio Fernando,Miguel Altamirano Cabrera,Dzmitry Tsetserukou*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需额外训练的多机器人导航架构AnyGoal，通过将视觉语言模型（VLM）整合入前沿探索流程，并利用2D高斯贝叶斯值图（BVM）协调多机器人协作，实现了在多任务场景中的领先性能，显著优于现有系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有端到端导航策略在跨场景/类别/任务目标迁移时性能下降；模块化导航管线受限于目标检测的召回率，而3D记忆系统则代价高昂且维护复杂。本工作旨在克服这些局限，提升导航系统在多样环境下的泛化能力。

Method: AnyGoal架构以视觉语言模型（VLM）为核心，结合前沿探索技术和2D高斯贝叶斯值图（BVM）进行信息累积，并通过精确加权的VLM得分进行贝叶斯更新，实现终身证据累积。前沿优先级基于VLM评判和贝叶斯UCB项加权融合。对机器人分配采用贪心分配器，具备空间分离惩罚和决策滞后机制，无需中心化控制。

Result: 在GOAT-Bench验证集未见分割上，双机器人AnyGoal系统在严格物理环境下达到了52.4%的子任务成功率（SR），12.7%的SPL，较Modular GOAT高出27.5个百分点。单机器人版本子任务SR为41.9%，证明多决策架构带来性能提升。感知消融实验表明开放式词汇检测器提升了探索效率，但目标验证成为新的主要瓶颈。

Conclusion: AnyGoal实现了无需训练的高效泛化导航，并突破了传统模块化和记忆系统的局限，在多机器人合作与终身学习探索中表现优异，成为物理约束下导航任务的新标杆。

Abstract: End-to-end navigation policies trained on large simulation corpora degrade sharply when transferred to out-of-distribution scenes, categories, or goal modalities. Modular pipelines such as Modular GOAT are bottlenecked by closed-set object detection recall, while 3D snapshot-memory systems (e.g. 3D-Mem) accumulate dense, view-dependent representations that are heavy to maintain. We present AnyGoal, a training-free multi-robot architecture that places a Vision-Language Model (VLM) at the core of frontier-based exploration and coordinates agents through a shared 2D Gaussian Bayesian Value Map (BVM). The BVM maintains a per-pixel (mu, sigma^2) posterior over goal relevance, updated via precision-weighted fusion of VLM scores through a depth-cone mask, and is never reset between subtasks, yielding lifelong evidence accumulation. Frontiers are ranked by a convex blend of a VLM-as-judge softmax and a Bayesian UCB term on the BVM. A greedy allocator with spatial-separation penalty and commitment hysteresis distributes frontiers across agents without a centralized controller. On the full GOAT-Bench val unseen split (360 episodes, 2,669 subtasks), our dual-agent system achieves 52.4% Subtask SR at 12.7% SPL--state of the art under the strict physical regime (discrete 0.25 m steps, no teleportation, 42 deg HFOV) and a +27.5 pp improvement over Modular GOAT (24.9%). Single-agent AnyGoal achieves 41.9% Subtask SR, showing gains arise from the decision architecture. A four-way perception ablation shows that open-vocabulary detectors shift the dominant failure mode from exploration to goal verification.

### [122] [Guided Diffusion with Distilled Vision-Language Reliability for Aerial Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13883)
*Ivan Valuev,Iana Zhura,Valerii Serpiva,Didar Seyidov,Dzmitry Tsetserukou*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于可靠性感知扩散模型的3D无人机自主导航方法，大幅提升了导航安全性和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统无人机导航方法将感知、建图、规划分为多个阶段，导致误差传播、时延增加，以及难以适应新环境。端到端生成模型虽然能将观测直接映射为轨迹，但受限于对不可靠观测的识别能力，易在玻璃、镜面、过曝等区域误判环境，从而影响导航安全。

Method: 方法通过感知数据和场景级可靠性热力图共同生成导航轨迹。该热力图由轻量网络生成，通过蒸馏大型视觉-语言模型实现实时、泛化能力强的可靠性评估；轨迹生成利用可微分的两阶段ESDF代价函数，把‘实体’障碍物和高不可靠区域视作同等障碍，提升在未知环境中的适应性。

Result: 在仿真和实物无人机实验中，该方法导航轨迹更安全，障碍穿越率从40.3%降至9.6%，穿越区域平均可靠性从0.588提升到0.925。仅移除可靠性部分，平均可靠性下降至0.783，显示该部分至关重要。蒸馏后系统运行速度达原始VL模型2倍。

Conclusion: 基于可靠性感知的扩散规划器能够大幅提升无人机导航安全性和泛化能力，实现了端到端生成模型在现实复杂环境下的实际落地。

Abstract: Autonomous UAV navigation is conventionally solved by pipelines that separate perception, mapping, and planning into distinct stages, which propagates errors, accumulates latency, and requires environment-specific retuning. End-to-end generative models remove these interfaces by mapping raw observations directly to trajectories, but inherit a subtle failure mode: trained on clean data, they cannot recognise when an observation is unreliable, and treat degraded regions such as glass, mirrors, and overexposed surfaces as valid evidence for planning. We present a reliability-aware diffusion planner for 3D UAV navigation. It conditions trajectory generation on the observation together with a scene-level reliability heatmap that marks where perception cannot be trusted, produced by a lightweight network that distils the open-vocabulary reasoning of a vision-language model within the real-time planning budget. To generalise to unseen environments without retraining, we steer the denoising process with a differentiable two-stage ESDF cost that treats physical obstacles from depth and virtual obstacles from highly unreliable regions on equal footing. In simulation and on a real quadrotor, our planner produces markedly safer trajectories than a state-of-the-art diffusion baseline, reducing the obstacle-violation rate from 40.3% to 9.6% and raising the mean reliability of traversed regions from 0.588 to 0.925. Ablating the reliability term alone drops mean reliability from 0.898 to 0.783, confirming it as the decisive component, while distillation runs the framework up to 2 times faster than the full vision-language model.

### [123] [PhysVLA: Towards Physically-Grounded VLA for Embodied Robotic Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13886)
*Namai Chandra,Shriram Damodaran,Lin Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为PhysVLA的物理感知增强模块，可以在不修改、不微调任何主流Vision-Language-Action (VLA)控制模型权重及结构的情况下，实时提升机器人操作任务的物理合理性和成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前主流VLA模型虽然能根据视觉和语言指导对机器人进行有效控制，但由于只依赖行为演示数据训练，缺乏对刚体动力学、接触约束等关键物理原理的显式约束，导致操作轨迹物理一致性差，最终引发更多失败和轨迹质量损失。该物理鸿沟限制了VLA模型在实际物理环境中的应用与泛化能力。

Method: PhysVLA作为一个推理时叠加于任意冻结VLA骨干网络之上的“即插即用”模块，截获模型生成的控制动作，只利用系统状态信息，应用双层校正：一是基于任务阶段的有限状态机对操作过程进行分段结构化，二是当动力学检测器发现运动不一致时触发欧拉-拉格朗日动力学门控修正，从而实现对物理一致性的动态实时增强。该方法无需任何模型重训练，推理时延极低。

Result: 在多种VLA模型（包括OpenVLA, Force-VLA, Generalist-VLA等）与多种仿真平台下（如7自由度Franka Panda手臂、Robosuite Lift仿真等），PhysVLA均显著提升了操作成功率（最高+17%）、稳定性（最高+19%）、轨迹效率（最高+15%）及抗突变鲁棒性（最高提升10倍）。在真实机器人平台的抓取-放置任务中，同样无需微调，成功率提升高达50%。

Conclusion: PhysVLA体系证明了具备物理感知的VLA模型可作为运行时可组合的拓展模块，且具有极强的模型和场景泛化能力，有望成为提升机器人智能体实际物理表现力的新范式。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models excel at mapping visual inputs and natural language instructions directly to robotic control policies. However, because they are trained primarily to fit behavioural demonstration data, they do not explicitly enforce fundamental physical principles such as rigid-body dynamics or contact constraints. This exposes a critical physics gap: standard temporal smoothing applied on top of single-step or chunked VLAs trades trajectory quality for added failures that short-term memory cannot resolve. To bridge this gap, we introduce PhysVLA (Physics-VLA), a plug-and-play, inference-time framework designed to wrap any frozen VLA backbone without retraining, fine-tuning, or weight access, with less than 1 ms of overhead per control step. PhysVLA intercepts the predicted control action, captures only the simulator or system state, and applies a dual-layered correction: (i) a phase-aware finite-state machine that structures discrete task segments (approach, grasp, transport, and place), and (ii) a selective Euler-Lagrange gate that activates only when a dynamics oracle detects kinodynamic inconsistency. Evaluated across OpenVLA, OpenVLA-OFT, Force-VLA, and Generalist-VLA on LIBERO-Spatial with a 7-DoF Franka Panda, the framework delivers absolute success rate increases of up to 17% and stability increases of up to 19% with no per-task regressions, improves trajectory efficiency by up to 15% across all four backbones, and shows up to a 10x improvement in trajectory jerk robustness on a Robosuite Lift cross-simulator sweep. We further validate the framework on a real Agilex Piper arm with a pick-and-place task, confirming that PhysVLA transfers to physical hardware without retraining, with success-rate improvements of up to 50%, establishing physical awareness as a composable, backbone-agnostic runtime module.

However, trajectory tracking far from equilibrium states remains largely unaddressed. We close this gap by demonstrating the first swing-up of a magnetically actuated inverted pendulum using the clinically-ready Navion eMNS. Although the inverted pendulum is not clinically relevant in itself, the proposed method utilizes torques and forces as control objectives, making it applicable to other magnetically actuated devices such as catheters and guidewires. Our approach combines trajectory optimization that accounts for internal eMNS dynamics with time-varying Linear Quadratic Regulator (LQR) state feedback and Iterative Learning Control (ILC), which leverages previous trial data and the system's dynamic model to progressively refine the feedforward command. While LQR alone fails due to the complex phenomena of magnetic actuation, ILC enables successful swing-up within six iterations. Furthermore, post-experimental analysis reveals that the learned ILC correction closely matches the torque discrepancy predicted by high-fidelity magnetic field model calibration, suggesting learning and adaptation as a promising tool to deal with uncertainties in electromagnetic actuation arising, e.g., from patient-specific physiological motion patterns and field model calibration inaccuracies.

Abstract: Recent Gaussian splatting (GS) methods have shown that scenes can be represented efficiently with optimisable Gaussians for high-quality reconstruction and rendering. In this paper, building on this principle, we introduce SplatlessDF, a continuous distance field (DF) mapping framework that uses anisotropic Gaussian elements from a spatial rather than photometric perspective. SplatlessDF directly parameterises the Gaussians and optimises to recover a differentiable DF, enabling distances and gradients to be queried in the spatial domain for downstream robotic tasks such as navigation. Furthermore, SplatlessDF can be coupled with 2D Gaussian splatting (2DGS), providing a unified framework based solely on Gaussian primitives that can learn continuous DF and surface models and supports photometric rendering. We consider two settings: a standalone DF-only formulation and a joint DF-rendering formulation coupled with 2DGS. Experiments show that the standalone formulation provides efficient and accurate distance and gradient queries, while the joint formulation improves rendering geometry and simultaneously models a continuous DF. These results highlight the potential of GS-style representations not only for surface modelling and rendering but also for mapping representations suited to robotic navigation.

### [127] [From Attacks to Curricula: Learnability-Guided Adversarial Training for Safe Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14032)
*Yuewen Mei,Tong Nie,Jie Sun,Haotian Shi,Wei Ma,Jian Sun*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: AlignADV是一种用于自动驾驶策略训练的对抗训练新框架，着重于生成可解决且与策略能力匹配的场景，从而提升效率和安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对抗训练方法在自动驾驶中常生成极端且无法解决的攻击性场景，削弱了学习效率，也不能适时适应策略能力提升；因此需要一种能动态对齐策略能力、提升训练有效性的新方法。

Method: AlignADV通过重塑场景生成问题为偏好对齐任务，利用偏好优化指导生成可攻克的关键场景，并引入行为指纹和能力预测模型，实现无须大量仿真即可动态预测策略表现，从而实现针对性场景采样以训练策略。

Result: 在Waymo开放数据集上，AlignADV相较于主流方法能减少高达40.6%的训练步数，并降低碰撞率、提升正常和对抗交通下的路径完成率。

Conclusion: AlignADV表明从攻击导向到可学性导向的训练范式，有助于提升自动驾驶策略的安全性与效率，为自动驾驶训练提供了更有原则性的新方向。

Abstract: Closed-loop adversarial training improves autonomous driving safety by exposing policies to rare safety-critical scenarios. Standard pipelines first generate adversarial scenarios and then sample them for policy optimization. However, most existing frameworks remain attack-oriented: collision-driven generators often synthesize unsolvable extreme situations, which can degrade learning, while heuristic samplers ignore the evolving capability of the driving policy, causing sample inefficiency and delayed convergence. We propose AlignADV, a learnability-guided closed-loop adversarial training framework that converts adversarial scenarios into resolvable and capability-aligned curricula. First, we reformulate adversarial scenario generation as a preference alignment problem and employ direct preference optimization to guide the generator toward critical yet resolvable scenarios. Second, we introduce behavioral fingerprints to capture the intrinsic characteristics of the evolving policy and construct a multi-modal capability prediction model that estimates policy performance without expensive closed-loop simulations. By combining resolvability-aligned scenarios with capability predictions, AlignADV develops a dynamic curriculum sampling mechanism that prioritizes scenarios targeting the current policy's vulnerabilities. Experiments on the Waymo Open Motion Dataset demonstrate that AlignADV improves convergence efficiency and final performance, reducing training steps by up to 40.6 percent compared with baseline methods while lowering collision rate and improving route completion under both normal and adversarial traffic conditions. These results highlight a shift from attack-oriented scenario generation to learnability-guided policy improvement, offering a principled direction for safer and more efficient autonomous driving training. Project page: https://meiyuewen.github.io/AlignADV/.

</details>


### [128] [ReactSim-Bench: Benchmarking Reactive Behavior World Model Simulation in Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14058)
*Zhiyuan Zhang,Yanlun Peng,Jianing Zhang,Xianda Guo,Zehan Huang,Haoran Liu,Qifeng Li,Shaofeng Zhang,Xiaosong Jia,Junchi Yan*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了针对自动驾驶仿真的行为世界模型反应能力评测基准ReactSim-Bench，通过独立控制自动驾驶车辆（AV）和周围智能体，系统性地评价现有主流模型的反应能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动驾驶仿真中的行为模拟评测，主要关注与日志的相似性或预测准确性，而未能直接衡量智能体对AV新行为的反应能力。模拟环境中如果不能合理应对与训练日志不同的AV行为，会影响自动驾驶安全性评估和模型泛化能力。

Method: 作者提出ReactSim-Bench：将AV与其他智能体的控制解耦，使用人工规划且与日志不同的AV行为作为输入，要求智能体做出合理反应。为此，设计了一条从AV规划模型生成行为、再通过规则与人工筛选验证的场景生成流水线。提出多种评价指标（碰撞率、地图规则遵循性、运动学可行性）评估系统反应的安全与合规性。最终共构建2636个测试场景，并对多种主流模型架构做系统评估。

Result: 利用ReactSim-Bench，作者对现有基于Transformer、扩散模型和下一个动作预测等多种架构的方法进行了全面测试与比较；同时探讨了重规划频率对反应性能的影响，为模型设计提供参考。

Conclusion: ReactSim-Bench实现了自动驾驶仿真中行为模型反应能力的系统性评测，为评价和改进自动驾驶行为模型提供了新基准，有助于提升仿真系统的泛化与安全性。

Abstract: Reactive capability is a key property of data-driven behavior world model simulators for autonomous driving simulation systems. With this capability, simulated world agents can respond feasibly to autonomous vehicle (AV) behaviors that differ from the log. However, existing behavior simulation benchmarks do not directly measure reactive capability. They often let the simulator jointly control the AV and surrounding agents and evaluate realism through log similarity or open-loop prediction metrics. In this work, we introduce ReactSim-Bench for evaluating the reactive capability of behavior world model simulation in autonomous driving. We decouple the control of agents and the AV, using AV behaviors that differ from the log and require agents to respond as independent AV inputs. To obtain these AV behaviors, we construct a pipeline that uses an AV planner model to generate candidate behaviors and filters the data using rules and manual verification. Collision metrics, map-based metrics, and kinematic feasibility metrics are used to evaluate the safety and rule compliance of reactive responses. We construct 2,636 test scenarios with three categories and conduct a systematic evaluation of state-of-the-art models across multiple architectures, including Transformer-based, diffusion-based, and next-token-prediction-based models. We further analyze how replan frequency affects performance and provide insights for future studies.

</details>


### [129] [Semidefinite Relaxations for Collision-Free Motion Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14063)
*Bernhard Paus Graesdal,Alexandre Amice,Pablo A. Parrilo,Russ Tedrake*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出利用半正定松弛（semidefinite relaxation）方法来解决点机器人在带有球形障碍物的n维空间中的无碰撞路径规划问题，并理论分析其紧性和计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无碰撞路径规划是机器人运动的重要难题，即使对简单的点机器人在球障碍物环境下，也具有高度非凸性和理论难度。目前对用半正定松弛方法求解此类问题的理论分析较少，相关松弛的松紧性、解释及效率还未明晰。

Method: 作者将路径规划建模为多项式曲线上的非凸优化问题，并提出相应的半正定松弛，并从几何角度解释松弛的等价性和松紧条件。此外，作者提出了对称性简化，使得半正定锥的规模仅与多项式次数线性相关、且与空间维数无关。最后，将该松弛用作RRT路径规划中的凸性牵引函数实现实际应用。

Result: 新提出的半正定松弛模型明显比传统非线性规划（如用SNOPT、IPOPT）速度快10-100倍，求解时间的方差显著降低，且能稳定找到原始问题的局部最优路径。实际在四旋翼最小抖动($C^4$连续)轨迹规划任务中，作为RRT（快速随机树）路径生成函数表现良好。

Conclusion: 该工作不仅首次理论分析了半正定松弛在无碰撞路径规划中的表现，明确了松弛紧性的直观几何条件，还提升了计算效率，验证了其实用性，对高维复杂机器人规划具有理论与应用指导意义。

Abstract: We study semidefinite relaxations for collision-free motion planning. We focus on a point robot moving from start to goal through spherical obstacles in $\mathbb{R}^n$, subject to path continuity constraints and squared derivative costs; a setting that is conceptually simple yet captures the hardness of collision-free motion planning. We formulate this problem exactly as a nonconvex problem over polynomial curves, and present a natural semidefinite relaxation. We contribute two key theoretical insights; to our knowledge this is the first theoretical analysis of semidefinite relaxations for collision-free motion planning. First, we show that solving the convex relaxation is equivalent to solving, to global optimality, a related motion planning problem in a potentially higher-dimensional space. This geometric interpretation yields necessary and sufficient conditions for tightness, and a clear intuition for when the relaxation is loose. Second, we show that the relaxation admits a symmetry reduction that makes it significantly smaller than one might expect, with positive semidefinite cone sizes that scale linearly with the polynomial degree and are independent of the ambient dimension. The resulting relaxation is 10 to 100 times faster than direct nonlinear programming transcriptions solved with SNOPT and IPOPT, exhibits significantly lower variance in solve times, and reliably finds a locally optimal path for the original problem. We demonstrate its effectiveness as a convex steering function in an RRT planner for minimum-snap quadrotor planning with $C^4$ continuous trajectories.

</details>

The coupled propulsion units feature a differential mechanism capable of posture changes via a single wire, enabling adaptation to pipe diameter variations. To traverse obstacles like pipe joints, a control method was devised that detects obstacle contact through current load on the drive wheel motors and slackens the wire. Our proposed control method significantly improved the step-over capability of the new articulated robots.

Method: 设计并实现了一种使用绞盘驱动装置的多指可穿戴手套，能够在手指端提供平面屈伸方向的力反馈。通过台架验证和含机器人手臂遥操作的用户实验，评估了其性能。

Abstract: Humans rely on directional fingertip forces to probe and regulate contact during manipulation, yet most wearable haptic gloves render only vibration or single-axis force, leaving force direction ambiguous. We present the N2D Haptic Glove, a multi-finger wearable device that renders planar flexion-extension fingertip forces using capstan-drive transmissions for high-transparency force feedback. Through benchtop validations and a user study involving haptic teleoperation of a robotic arm and hand, we demonstrate that compared to visual-only and single-axis haptic baselines, planar fingertip feedback significantly reduces contact force error during precise manipulation, improves trial-to-trial consistency, and enhances overall user experience in axial probing tasks. These findings establish the N2D Haptic Glove and directional finger-based haptics devices as a promising modality for contact-rich teleoperation, immersive virtual reality simulations, and robot learning from demonstrations. Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需额外训练，在测试时通过选择扩散噪声（SDN）提升机器人视觉-语言-动作（VLA）策略鲁棒性和成功率的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散式VLA策略在泛化能力上强大，但对无关视觉相关性和动作噪声敏感，导致在真实扰动下表现脆弱。因此亟需机制提升其鲁棒性和稳定性。

Method: 提出Selected Diffusion Noise (SDN)方法，在测试阶段动态采样与参考集合最大分离的噪声向量，规避虚假线索，结合动作轨迹连贯性筛选候选，达到稳健的动作输出，无需更改模型参数。

Result: 在Google Robot、Widow-X仿真平台，以及两个真实机器人数据集上，SDN在多种VLA策略中均带来约8%（仿真）和10%（真实）的成功率提升，同时输出动作更平滑、稳定。

Conclusion: 扩散噪声的选择是一种通用且有效的、可直接在测试时加强VLA策略鲁棒性和性能的方法，有助于推动此类方法在真实场景中的可靠应用。

Abstract: Diffusion-based Vision-Language-Action (VLA) policies enable strong generalization in robotic manipulation, but remain sensitive to spurious visual correlations and noisy action generation, leading to brittle behavior under perturbations. We introduce Selected Diffusion Noise (SDN), a simple, training-free test-time method that improves both robustness and success rate by leveraging the diffusion noise space as a controllable degree of freedom. SDN dynamically samples noise vectors that are maximally separated from a reference set to mitigate reliance on spurious cues, while selecting candidates that yield more coherent action trajectories. This dual objective encourages stable behavior even under object-masked observations and reduces action jitter without modifying model parameters. We evaluate SDN on two simulation benchmarks (Google Robot, Widow-X) and two real-world robotic datasets across multiple VLA policies, including pi_0, Groot-N1.5, and Groot-N1.6. SDN consistently improves success rates by +8% in simulation and +10% in real-world settings, while producing smoother and more stable actions. Our results highlight that diffusion noise selection can serve as an effective and general mechanism for enhancing VLA policies at test time.

### [133] [A Modular Dual-Arm Apple Harvesting Robot with Enhanced Field Performance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14089)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Compared to our prior horizontal dual-arm system, the platform integrates 5 advances: (1)a foundation-model-based perception pipeline combining Grounding-DINO and EfficientViT-SAM for robust fruit localization in unstructured outdoor environments; (2)7th-order jerk-bounded trajectory generation paired with a Control Barrier Function safety filter to achieve fast yet safe arm motions; (3)a linear sweep harvesting strategy with a 10cm approach buffer and rotational detachment that improves picking reliability; (4)a temporal-logic-based dual-arm coordination policy with vision-arm async scheduling that maximizes usage of a shared vacuum source; and (5)field validation in 2 commercial orchards covering different apple varieties and tree architectures during the 2025 harvest season. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统本体状态估计算法通常将所有传感器测量值拼接为一个向量，无法灵活反映各数据的重要性，且基于接触辅助的方法还需显式模型脚部接触，适应性不足。现有学习型估计算法也未充分利用传感器及接触信息之间的复杂关系。

Method: 将惯性与各腿传感器数据分别编码为token，输入带有注意力机制的网络，让网络学习每种传感器数据在不同地形、动作下的重要性分布，无需传统的显式接触判别器或测量更新流程。

Result: 在Unitree Go1机器人上，面对模拟中未建模的复杂地面和未见过的步态时，本文方法较现有学习型算法和基于接触模型的方法都取得了更优的状态估计效果。

Abstract: In this paper, we propose a method that applies Inertial-Leg (IL) tokenization to an attention-based network for proprioceptive state estimation in legged robots. Unlike existing learning-based state estimators that concatenate all sensor measurements into a single flat vector, the proposed architecture represents inertial measurements and leg-wise measurements as individual tokens and uses an attention mechanism to learn the relative importance of each measurement.This design allows the network to reweight each measurement according to the current contact condition, reflecting the fact that the reliability of forward kinematic measurements depends on whether the corresponding foot is in contact. Unlike conventional contact-aided estimators, however, the proposed method learns this behavior without relying on an explicit contact estimator or on explicit measurement updates based on a stationary contact assumption. To validate the proposed method, we conducted experiments on a Unitree Go1 robot, including debris terrain not modeled in simulation and gait patterns not seen during training. Experimental results show that the proposed method achieves better estimation performance than existing learning-based state estimators under unseen gait patterns and also improves performance over contact-aided model-based methods.

### [135] [Robustness without Wrinkles: Parallel Simulation and Robust MPC for Certified Deformable Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14188)
*Wei-Chen Li,Jeffrey Fang,Sasanka Polisetti,Yuexi Song,Glen Chou*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 核心为一种基于GPU并行的可微分仿真器，结合接触平滑技术，支持高效的基于梯度的规划。采用基于GPU并行的输出反馈鲁棒模型预测控制（MPC），增强约束满足性。同时借助共形预测对视觉反馈和感知误差进行校准，提升现实世界中的鲁棒性和安全性。此外，该仿真器还能加速模型基础的强化学习。

Result: CORD-SLS在仿真和真实硬件的高维、多接触绳索与布料操作任务（如避障、布线、折叠、平整）中均进行了评估。实验显示其实现了毫秒级规划速度，在安全性、执行速度和任务完成率方面超越现有基线方法。

Conclusion: CORD-SLS是一种高效且鲁棒的控制框架，适合应用于安全至关重要的可变形物体操作任务，在速度与安全性方面具有明显优势。

Abstract: We present CORD-SLS, a real-time control method for safe deformable object manipulation, with a focus on ropes and cloth. At its core is a GPU-parallel differentiable simulator with contact smoothing which enables efficient gradient-based planning through intermittent contact. To robustly satisfy constraints under model and sensing uncertainty, we develop a real-time, GPU-parallel output-feedback robust model predictive control (MPC) algorithm that plans with this simulator. We further show that the simulator accelerates model-based RL for training neural manipulation policies. To improve real-world robustness, we use conformal prediction to calibrate visual-feedback and perception-error bounds for MPC, producing reachable tubes that enable high-probability safe control. We evaluate CORD-SLS on high-dimensional, contact-rich rope and cloth manipulation tasks in simulation and hardware, including obstacle avoidance, routing, folding, and smoothing. Across settings, CORD-SLS achieves millisecond-speed planning, exceeding baselines in safety, speed, and task success.

</details>

We demonstrate that this combination of capabilities enables learning bimanual, whole-body, and active compliant policies that operate effectively in highly constrained spaces. The learned robust autonomous policies achieve high success rates across a variety of tasks, including long-horizon mobile manipulation, force-mediated box flipping, visually occluded box pushing, and space-constrained tabletop manipulation. Videos, code, and additional information can be found at https://ume-exo.github.io.

### [138] [Selective Agentic Recovery for UAV Autonomy with a Persistent Mission Runtime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14219)
*Taewoo Park,Kyeonghyun Yoo,Seunghyun Yoo,Hwangnam Kim*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一个名为PMR的无人机自主恢复框架，通过在关键时刻按需调用外部智能推理，实现高效、安全地处理飞行任务中的异常情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 面对无人机本地自主控制在遭遇障碍或任务歧义时处理能力有限、难以灵活决策的问题，需要高层次智能推理辅助，但频繁调用外部智能会带来延迟和成本，因此只有在必要时激活才最有价值。

Method: 提出了PMR框架，将任务循环与安全关键操作保持在本地，仅在需要时调用外部agentic reasoner作为恢复模块。引入learned-CVI（认知调用价值），基于学习方法判断是否值得激活远程推理。推理返回的决策在本地经过验证、安全过滤和动作映射，以确保飞行安全。

Result: 在400次8类场景的标准化Gazebo/PX4仿真基准测试中，learned-CVI方法将复杂环境下无人机任务成功率从本地自主的5.0%提升至95.0%，比单次和周期调用基线分别高20.0和32.5个百分点，且远程推理调用次数减少16.7%，日志token数减少29.2%。

Conclusion: PMR框架结合了本地自主与按需智能推理，有效提升了无人机在复杂任务中的恢复能力和成功率，同时控制了资源消耗。learned-CVI门控机制使得只有在有显著收益时才引入外部智能，大幅优化了系统性能。

Abstract: Agentic AI can support unmanned aerial vehicle (UAV) autonomy by providing high-level recovery reasoning when local waypoint- or setpoint-based execution encounters blocked passages, repeated no-progress behavior, or mission-level ambiguity. On physical UAVs, however, remote reasoning is most useful when it is invoked selectively, since each call introduces latency, resource cost, backend uncertainty, and a need to validate the returned decision. This paper presents Persistent Mission Runtime (PMR), a UAV recovery framework that keeps the mission loop and safety-critical execution local while using an external agentic reasoner only as an on-demand recovery module. The reasoner selects from predefined recovery skills, and each returned decision is parsed, verified, safety-filtered, and mapped to local executor actions before it can affect flight. PMR introduces learned Cognitive Value of Invocation (learned-CVI), a compact admission gate that estimates when remote agentic reasoning is likely to improve near-term mission progress enough to justify its operational cost. Across a fixed 400-run Gazebo/PX4 benchmark with eight scenarios, learned-CVI raises hard/ambiguous-regime success from 5.0% under local-only autonomy to 95.0%, outperforms one-shot and periodic reasoning baselines by 20.0 and 32.5 percentage points, and reduces remote-agent calls by 16.7% and logged tokens by 29.2% relative to a manually tuned rule-based invocation baseline.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了BIM-Loc方法，核心包括：1）多重射线投射策略，实现高效的BIM点数据关联和3D观测到2D纹理空间的投影；2）结合BIM约束的位姿图优化框架，实现里程计、序列扫描与BIM结构的一致性；3）层次化贝叶斯推断模块，支持从像素到结构层的连续2D表面差异检测与更新。

Result: 在仿真与真实世界实验中，BIM-Loc在定位精度和鲁棒性方面明显优于现有的基于地图的方法。

Abstract: Accurate and robust localization is a fundamental requirement for service and inspection robots, particularly in feature-sparse indoor environments where traditional systems struggle due to a lack of distinct landmarks. While prior maps can enhance robustness, precise and compact maps capturing real-world details are often unavailable for new or frequently changing environments. This paper presents BIM-Loc, a novel discrepancy-aware LiDAR-based localization method that directly integrates Building Information Models (BIM) from the design phase. BIM-Loc simultaneously estimates trajectories aligned with the BIM coordinate system and identifies discrepancies between real-world observations and the as-designed BIM in an online fashion. Our core contributions include: (1) a novel multi-hit ray casting strategy for efficient BIM-point data association and projection of 3D observations into 2D texture space; (2) a pose graph optimization framework with BIM-integrated factors that enforces consistency among odometry, sequential scans, and BIM structures; and (3) a hierarchical Bayesian inference module that incrementally updates a continuous 2D surface representation for discrepancy detection, propagating updates from the pixel to the structure level. Extensive evaluations in both simulation and real-world applications demonstrate that BIM-Loc significantly outperforms state-of-the-art map-based methods in localization accuracy and robustness.

### [140] [When and How Severely: Scenario-Specific Safety Envelopes for Driving VLAs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14238)
*Abhinaw Priyadershi,Jelena Frtunikj*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文分析并认证了一种基于视觉-语言-行为（VLA）的自动驾驶决策规划器（Alpamayo R1），揭示单一安全门槛难以充分反映不同场景下的高危失败分布，提出需要二维安全包络用于安全认证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自动驾驶安全认证方法通常使用单一指标或门槛来衡量决策系统的表现，这可能掩盖某些情况下严重失效的风险。本研究旨在提出更细致与准确的安全分析框架，以满足ISO 21448（SOTIF）标准要求。

Method: 作者评估了一个10B参数的开源自动驾驶VLA模型（Alpamayo R1），在15968对(clip, attack)样本上测试表现，利用高斯混合模型（GMM）分析失效严重程度，探索不同场景下容忍失效的能力及高风险失效的分布特点。

Result: 发现单一平均误差门槛（如σ≤50时15% ADE）会掩盖个别场景的严重失效，GMM分析识别了六种失效严重度带。某些场景即使能容忍较大扰动噪声（如STOP_SIGNAL），其高危失败比例（C4/C5）仍明显高于其他任务（如LANE_KEEPING）。

Conclusion: 推动自动驾驶决策规划器的SOTIF安全认证时，需构建二维安全包络而非单一指标，以合理描述不同风险场景下的系统表现，从而提升安全规范的科学性和实用性。

Abstract: Safety certification of Vision-Language-Action (VLA) driving planners under ISO 21448 (SOTIF) rests on an Operational Design Domain (ODD) specification that answers two complementary questions: when does the planner start to fail, and how severely does it fail once it does? We evaluate Alpamayo R1, a 10B-parameter open-weight driving VLA, on 15,968 (clip, attack) pairs. We find a conservative-aggregate gap: an aggregate safe threshold of $σ\leq 50$ under a 15% average displacement error (ADE) budget masks well-sampled scenarios that tolerate the top of the tested grid ($σ= 70$). A Gaussian Mixture Model (GMM) on the changed-explanation subset identifies six discrete severity bands (BIC-optimal $k{=}6$), so two perturbation conditions with the same mean error can differ materially in their share of high-severity (C4/C5) failures. Joining the two analyses on the same corpus surfaces a finding neither yields in isolation: the scenarios with the loosest noise thresholds are not those with the lowest high-severity rate: STOP_SIGNAL concentrates roughly $4\times$ the C4/C5 share of LANE_KEEPING despite tolerating a larger $σ$. A deployable SOTIF ODD specification for driving VLAs therefore requires a two-dimensional safety envelope, not a single aggregate value per hazard.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有仿人机械手结构复杂、造价高或功能有限，难以兼顾外观、运动能力及实现成本，限制了其实用性。作者借鉴人体协同运动特性，试图以更简单的机制实现复杂的手部功能。

Method: 通过手势捕捉技术分析人手运动协同关系，优化DOF配置，并设计基于连杆的机械结构，用于协调多关节运动，具体包括一种新颖的球面四连杆，以在小型结构下实现掌指关节的两自由度运动。

Abstract: Designing anthropomorphic robotic hands that balance functional dexterity with mechanical simplicity remains a significant challenge. Inspired by human hand synergies, this paper presents the SyLink Hand, an anthropomorphic dexterous hand that integrates biomechanical synergy principles with linkage-driven transmission mechanisms to achieve a high degree of anthropomorphism in appearance, kinematics, and functionality within a compact and cost-effective architecture. Biomechanical analysis of natural hand motions using motion capture gloves reveals strong kinematic correlations among hand joints, providing the basis for a simplified yet functional degree-of-freedom (DOF) configuration. Guided by these synergistic characteristics, optimized linkage mechanisms are employed to coordinate multiple joint motions and reproduce natural finger trajectories. A novel spherical four-bar linkage is further proposed to achieve decoupled flexion/extension (Flex/Ext) and abduction/adduction (Abd/Add) at the metacarpophalangeal joint within a compact form factor. The resulting prototype integrates 19 joints driven by 11 actuators, with a total mass of 520g and a manufacturing cost of approximately USD 400. Experimental evaluations demonstrate its human-like kinematic performance, high load-bearing capability, and versatile grasping and manipulation skills. These results validate that the synergy-inspired, linkage-based design effectively balances anthropomorphism, mechanical simplicity, and functional versatility, highlighting its potential for practical deployment in dexterity-demanding robotic applications.

### [142] [Optimality-Preserving Decomposition for Scalable QAOA in Natural-Language-Guided Multi-Drone Assignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14252)
*Junyeop Bang,Byongho Lee,Dohyun An,Hwangnam Kim*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种结合大语言模型（LLM）与量子-经典混合优化来解决多无人机分区分派问题的端到端新框架。该方法能高效将自然语言指令转化为可在受限量子硬件上求解的优化约束，并在大规模任务分配中优于传统算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着多无人机任务分配问题规模扩大，传统穷举方法无法解决NP困难的分区分派组合问题。尽管量子优化具备潜力，但因硬件受限和任务表达复杂，难以直接利用。因此，作者希望用新的架构实现从人类意图到量子优化硬件的高效映射，突破规模瓶颈。

Method: 提出了一套端到端体系：前端以SFT（有监督微调）和DPO优化的大语言模型，将自然语言指令精准转为QUBO优化约束；后端通过新颖的保约束图划分策略和压缩分隔-动态规划融合，适应有限量子比特资源；优化过程中用W态初始化和XY-mixer嵌入CVaR-QAOA，使约束结构紧凑高效。

Result: 实验证明，在理想化oracle场景下可100%找回全局最优解，真实量子采样下达96.3%，且大规模无人机分配时有效突破传统算法规模瓶颈。

Conclusion: 该方法显著提升了多无人机、复杂空间任务的自然语言分派效率和规模，拓展了量子计算实际应用边界，为自动化决策分配系统提供了新方向。

Abstract: As multi-drone fleets scale, zone assignment rapidly evolves into an intractable NP-hard combinatorial problem that overwhelms classical exhaustive search. While quantum optimization promises to shatter these classical bottlenecks, mapping complex spatial tasks from human intent to restricted quantum hardware remains a severe challenge. To bridge this gap, we present an end-to-end framework integrating a fine-tuned Large Language Model (LLM) front-end with a highly scalable, domain-specific quantum-classical backend. The front-end utilizes Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) and Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) to translate free-form natural language instructions into structurally robust Quadratic Unconstrained Binary Optimization (QUBO) constraints without false negatives. To overcome the strict qubit limits of near-term quantum devices, our framework features a novel constraint-preserving graph partitioner and a compressed separator-based dynamic programming (DP) merge. By structurally encoding constraints via W-state initialization and XY-mixers in Conditional Value-at-Risk Quantum Approximate Optimization (CVaR-QAOA), the pipeline stays highly compact. Empirical results demonstrate that this architecture circumvents classical scaling walls, recovering the global optimum on 100% of idealized oracle cases and 96.3% under real QAOA sampling, enabling natural-language-guided task allocation at previously intractable scales.

### [143] [ReactVLA: Fast and Lightweight Reactive Robot Manipulation via Improved Mean Flow Action Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14255)
*Yanzhao Guo,Wenkai Chen,Jianwei Zhang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了ReactVLA，一种低延迟的视觉-语言-动作（VLA）框架，用于实现实时机器人操作。该方法结合了快速动作生成和动态特征路由，大幅度提升了推理速度和任务表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散式VLA策略虽表现优异，但推理速度慢，限制了其实时机器人操作中的应用。因此，提升VLA模型在机器人操作中的实时性成为亟需解决的问题。

Method: ReactVLA方法由两方面组成：其一是改进版的Mean Flow（iMF）动作生成器，将多步扩散采样简化为一到几步动作生成，其二是引入Attention Residuals（AttnRes），用动态深度特征路由机制取代均匀残差累积，更好地保留任务相关的多模态信息。

Result: ReactVLA在大规模仿真基准（如LIBERO和RoboIMI）及真实机器人任务上的实验显示，其性能和速度均优于同尺寸VLA方法（如SmolVLA和π_0）。在高精度操作任务中，表现提升高达1.65倍，推理速度提升超过4倍，延迟降低至38.6毫秒内。

Conclusion: ReactVLA大大提升了VLA模型在机器人实时操作中的适用性，为真实物理平台上的反应式控制提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Diffusion-based Vision-Language-Action (VLA) policies have demonstrated strong capability in modeling expressive and multimodal action distributions. However, their reliance on iterative sampling introduces substantial inference latency, which limits their applicability to reactive closed-loop robot manipulation. To address this limitation, we propose \texttt{ReactVLA}, a lightweight and low-latency VLA framework for real-time robotic manipulation. \texttt{ReactVLA} combines two complementary designs: (1) an improved Mean Flow (iMF) action generator that reduces expensive multi-step diffusion sampling to one-to-few-step action generation, and (2) Attention Residuals (AttnRes), a dynamic depth-wise feature routing mechanism that replaces uniform residual accumulation to better preserve task-relevant multimodal representations. We evaluate \texttt{ReactVLA} on large-scale simulation benchmarks, including LIBERO and RoboIMI, as well as real-world robotic manipulation tasks. Experimental results show that \texttt{ReactVLA} consistently outperforms similarly sized VLA baselines, including SmolVLA and $π_0$. On challenging precision manipulation tasks, \texttt{ReactVLA} achieves up to a 1.65$\times$ improvement in task performance while providing more than a 4$\times$ increase in inference speed compared with leading VLA models. Finally, it reduces real-world policy latency to below 38.6 ms, enabling fast reactive control on physical robot platforms. Please check out our project website at: https://game-loader.github.io/ReactVLA/.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前大多基于平面图的导航研究主要聚焦于PointNav任务且覆盖的环境有限，缺少融合多种任务和大规模数据支持的方法与验证。为弥补该领域的不足，本文提出了整合PointNav、ObjectNav和ImageNav的统一新任务。

Method: 1) 构建了FloVerse-1.6K数据集，包含1600个场景及对应平面图，涵盖24万条专家轨迹和1200万RGBD帧；2) 提出TwoDiff导航策略，包括基于扩散模型的多模态模块进行目标推理和基于深度的轨迹优化模块，实现安全执行。

Result: 实验显示：1) 利用场景结构的空间先验能在三种不同目标类型导航中均提升性能；2) ThreeDiff能够隐式捕获并利用平面图所提供的空间信息。

Conclusion: 空间先验（如平面图）能够增强智能体的导航能力，提出的数据集和方法能够有效统一并推动具身导航多任务发展。

Abstract: Floor plans encapsulate compact spatial priors, enabling agents to navigate unseen scenes more efficiently. While prior work has explored floor plan-guided navigation, it has focused mainly on PointNav and a limited set of environments. To bridge this gap, we introduce FloVerse, a new task for floor plan-guided embodied navigation that unifies PointNav, ObjectNav, and ImageNav. To support FloVerse, we assemble FloVerse-1.6K, a large-scale dataset of 1.6K scenes from HM3D and Gibson 4+, paired with corresponding floor plans, comprising 240K expert trajectories and 12M RGBD frames. We further propose ThreeDiff, a two-stage imitation learning policy comprising a planner, a diffusion-based multimodal goal-reasoning module trained via masked-modality modeling, and a refiner, a depth-based trajectory-refinement module for safe execution. Extensive experiments demonstrate that (1) floor-plan priors improve navigation performance across all goal modalities, and (2) ThreeDiff implicitly captures spatial information from floor plans. These results underscore the effectiveness of spatial priors and validate our proposed unified approach for floor plan-guided embodied navigation.
